1968, c.6, s.349; 1973, c.52, s.4; [1974, c.22](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-1974-c-22/latest/snb-1974-c-22.html)(Supp.), [s.7](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#sec7_smooth); [1980, c.27, s.8](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-1980-c-27/latest/snb-1980-c-27.html); [1982, c.32, s.3](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-1982-c-32/latest/snb-1982-c-32.html); [1987, c.6, s.45](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-1987-c-6/latest/snb-1987-c-6.html); [1988, c.20, s.1](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-1988-c-20/latest/snb-1988-c-20.html); [1993, c.22, s.1](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-1993-c-22/latest/snb-1993-c-22.html); [2008, c.2, s.16](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2008-c-2/latest/snb-2008-c-2.html); [2013, c.31, s.20](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2013-c-31/latest/snb-2013-c-31.html); [2015, c.30, s.4](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2015-c-30/latest/snb-2015-c-30.html); [2016, c.36, s.7](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2016-c-36/latest/snb-2016-c-36.html); [2017, c.48, s.9](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2017-c-48/latest/snb-2017-c-48.html); [2021, c.8, s.50](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

Repealed

[353](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)Repealed: [2015, c.30, s.5](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2015-c-30/latest/snb-2015-c-30.html)

1968, c.6, s.350; [2008, c.2, s.17](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2008-c-2/latest/snb-2008-c-2.html); [2013, c.31, s.20](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2013-c-31/latest/snb-2013-c-31.html); 2015, c.30, s.5

SPECIAL INSURANCE BROKER’S LICENCE

[2021, c.8, s.51](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

Special insurance broker’s licence

[2021, c.8, s.52](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

[354(1)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)The Superintendent may issue to any suitable person a licence to act as a special insurance broker to negotiate, continue or renew contracts of insurance with insurers not authorized to transact the business of insurance in the Province.

[354(2)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)Before being issued a licence under subsection (1), an applicant shall execute and deliver to the Superintendent security to the satisfaction of the Superintendent in an amount not less than $5,000 that the licensee will faithfully comply with all the requirements of this Act and the regulations or any other Act of the Legislature.

1968, c.6, s.351; [1971, c.41, s.15](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-1971-c-41/latest/snb-1971-c-41.html); [2008, c.2, s.18](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2008-c-2/latest/snb-2008-c-2.html); [2013, c.31, s.20](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2013-c-31/latest/snb-2013-c-31.html); [2015, c.30, s.6](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2015-c-30/latest/snb-2015-c-30.html); [2017, c.48, s.9](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2017-c-48/latest/snb-2017-c-48.html); [2021, c.8, s.53](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

Negotiation, continuation or renewal of insurance by a special insurance broker

[2021, c.8, s.54](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

[354.1](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)A holder of a special insurance broker licence may negotiate, continue or renew all classes of insurance, other than life insurance, accident insurance, sickness insurance, automobile insurance or a class of insurance prescribed by regulation.

[2021, c.8, s.54](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

Arranging insurance with unlicensed insurers

[2021, c.8, s.55](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

[355(1)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#) Subject to subsection (2), a special insurance broker may assist or act on behalf of a person who wishes to enter into or renew an insurance contract with an unlicensed insurer if

(a)
sufficient insurance cannot be arranged with an insurer licensed to do business in the Province,

(b)
sufficient insurance cannot be arranged at reasonable rates with an insurer licensed to do business in the Province, or

(c)
sufficient insurance cannot be arranged on the terms required by the insured with an insurer licensed to do business in the Province.

[355(2)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)Before a person enters into or renews an insurance contract, a special insurance broker shall obtain from the applicant a written statement that

(a)
is dated and signed by the applicant,

(b)
describes fully the nature and the amount of the insurance the applicant requires,

(c)
states that

(i)
the insurance cannot be obtained from licensed insurers in the Province, obtained at reasonable rates from licensed insurers in the Province or obtained on the terms required by the insured from licensed insurers in the Province, and

(ii)
the application for the insurance at the stated rate of premium was previously made to and refused by named insurers licensed in the Province, and

(d)
contains any further information that the Superintendent may require.

[355(3)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)Before a person enters into or renews an insurance contract, a special insurance broker shall advise the applicant, in writing, of the following:

(a)
that the unlicensed insurer is not regulated under this Act;

(b)
that the Superintendent has no authority under this Act with respect to the unlicensed insurer;

(c)
that the orderly payment of claims may be more difficult than it would be if the applicant obtained insurance from an insurer licensed under this Act;

(d)
that the applicant may not have the protection of any compensation plan operated by a compensation association designated under the regulations;

(e)
that the applicant may have to take legal proceedings in a foreign jurisdiction to enforce the contract of insurance; and

(f)
any other information that the Superintendent considers necessary.

[355(4)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)Every special insurance broker shall keep a separate record of insurance entered into or renewed by the special insurance broker under the licence in the form the Superintendent requires and shall make those records available for inspection by the Superintendent.

[355(5)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)Within 10 days after the end of each month, every special insurance broker shall make a return to the Superintendent, in the form and manner the Superintendent requires, containing particulars of all insurance effected by the special insurance broker during the month and provide any other information required by the Superintendent.

[355(6)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)In respect of all premiums on insurance effected under a special insurance broker’s licence, the special insurance broker shall pay to the Province any taxes as would be payable if the premiums had been received by a licensed insurer, and payment for the taxes shall accompany the monthly return under subsection (5).

1968, c.6, s.352; [2008, c.11, s.14](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2008-c-11/latest/snb-2008-c-11.html); [2021, c.8, s.56](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

Release or cancellation of security

[2021, c.8, s.57](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

[356](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)When the Superintendent is satisfied that all insurances effected by a licensed special insurance broker are no longer in force or have been reinsured and that the taxes owing to the Province have been paid, the special insurance broker is entitled to a release or cancellation of the security referred to in [subsection 354(2)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#sec354subsec2_smooth).

1968, c.6, s.353; [2013, c.31, s.20](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2013-c-31/latest/snb-2013-c-31.html); [2021, c.8, s.58](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

Unlawful contracts of insurance

[357(1)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)A special insurance broker licensed under this Act shall accept applications for insurance with unlicensed insurers only from the insured, a licensed agent or another licensed special insurance broker and shall not pay or allow compensation or anything of value in respect of the application to any person not licensed as an agent or special insurance broker under this Act.

[357(2)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)A contract of insurance with an unlicensed insurer made by or through an agent not licensed as a special insurance broker under this Act shall be considered unlawfully made within the meaning of section 369.

[357(3)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)If an insurance contract is not made or cancelled due to a special insurance broker’s failure or neglect to remit a premium to the insurer, the special insurance broker shall be personally liable to the insured or intended insured in the same manner as if the insurance contract had been made or not cancelled and the special insurance broker was the insurer.

1968, c.6, s.354; [2021, c.8, s.59](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

TEMPORARY AUTHORIZATIONS

[2021, c.8, s.60](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

Temporary authorization

[2021, c.8, s.61](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

[358](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)Subject to the terms and conditions that the Superintendent considers appropriate, the Superintendent may issue a temporary authorization to an adjuster from another jurisdiction to act within the Province when, in the opinion of the Superintendent, an emergency situation requires that the adjuster be granted the authorization.

1968, c.6, s.355; [1974, c.22](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-1974-c-22/latest/snb-1974-c-22.html)(Supp.), [s.8](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#sec8_smooth); [2013, c.31, s.20](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2013-c-31/latest/snb-2013-c-31.html); [2015, c.30, s.7](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2015-c-30/latest/snb-2015-c-30.html); [2017, c.48, s.9](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2017-c-48/latest/snb-2017-c-48.html); [2021, c.8, s.62](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

DAMAGE APPRAISERS

[2021, c.8, s.63](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

Damage appraisers

[2021, c.8, s.64](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

[358.1(1)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)An insurance company or an adjusting firm that uses the services of a damage appraiser shall ensure that the damage appraiser has the appropriate qualifications and competency to appraise any insurance claim that the damage appraiser is involved in on behalf of the insurance company or adjusting firm, as the case may be, and shall oversee the activities of the damage appraiser with respect to any insurance claim.

[358.1(2)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)If the Superintendent is of the opinion, on reasonable grounds, that a damage appraiser does any of the following, the Superintendent, after providing the damage appraiser an opportunity to be heard, may prohibit the damage appraiser from acting as a damage appraiser under this Act:

(a)
violated or failed to comply with a written undertaking made by the damage appraiser under this Act or the regulations;

(b)
committed a fraudulent act or practice;

(c)
committed any of the prohibited acts referred to in subsection (3);

(d)
demonstrated incompetency or untrustworthiness; or

(e)
is otherwise unsuitable.

[358.1(3)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)In the appraisal of any insurance claim, a damage appraiser shall not

(a)
possess any interest in the property the damage appraiser is engaged to appraise,

(b)
seek to make a profit or seek or acquire an interest, other than fees or salary, in the property the damage appraiser is engaged to appraise,

(c)
knowingly report the need to replace parts when the parts are repairable in a satisfactory manner, or agree or conspire with a garage, body shop or other repair facility to replace parts when the parts are repairable in a satisfactory manner,

(d)
act or attempt to act as an adjuster in connection with a property the damage appraiser is appraising,

(e)
fail or refuse to comply with any standards of practice and duties prescribed by regulation for damage appraisers, or

(f)
fail or refuse to comply with or contravene a provision of this Act or the regulations.

[1976, c.34, s.6](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-1976-c-34/latest/snb-1976-c-34.html); [1978, c.30, s.7](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-1978-c-30/latest/snb-1978-c-30.html); [2008, c.2, s.19](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2008-c-2/latest/snb-2008-c-2.html); [2013, c.31, s.20](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2013-c-31/latest/snb-2013-c-31.html); [2015, c.30, s.8](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2015-c-30/latest/snb-2015-c-30.html); [2017, c.48, s.9](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2017-c-48/latest/snb-2017-c-48.html); [2021, c.8, s.65](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

APPEALS

[2021, c.8, s.66](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

Appeals

[2021, c.8, s.66](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/astat/snb-2021-c-8/latest/snb-2021-c-8.html)

[358.2(1)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)A decision of the Superintendent referred to below may be appealed to the [Tribunal](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/snb-2013-c-30/latest/snb-2013-c-30.html) within 30 days after the date of the decision:

(a)
refusing to issue, renew or reinstate a licence under this Part;

(b)
suspending or revoking a licence under this Part;

(c)
imposing a term and condition on a licence under this Part;

(d)
prohibiting an individual from soliciting, negotiating, selling or arranging insurance on behalf of a restricted insurance representative under [subsection 352(26)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#sec352subsec26_smooth);

(e)
prohibiting a damage appraiser from acting as a damage appraiser under this Act; or

(f)
any other decision prescribed by regulation.

[358.2(2)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)Despite subsection (1), the [Tribunal](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/snb-2013-c-30/latest/snb-2013-c-30.html) may extend the period for appealing a decision, before or after the expiration of the time, if it is satisfied that there are reasonable grounds for an extension.

Insurer to maintain compliance system

(a)

(b)
an adjusting firm;

(c)
an agency;

(d)
an agent;

(e)

(g)

(h)

[361.2(1)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)An insurer that authorizes any of the persons referred to in paragraphs 361.1(a) to (h) to act on the insurer’s behalf shall notify the Superintendent in writing if the insurer has reasonable grounds to believe that a person who acts on behalf of the insurer is not suitable to carry on business authorized under the licence.

[361.2(2)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)The notice referred to in subsection (1) shall be given within 15 days after the insurer determines that there are reasonable grounds to believe that the person is not suitable to carry on business authorized under the licence.

Money in trust to be held in trust account

[364(1)](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)When the following persons receive trust money, the person shall have at least one account for deposits and the account shall be designated as a trust account both in the books of the person and in the records of the institution:

Return

[365](https://www.canlii.org/en/nb/laws/stat/rsnb-1973-c-i-12/latest/rsnb-1973-c-i-12.html#)Every agent, managing general agent, restricted insurance representative and third party administrator and every insurer shall make a return to the Superintendent, in the form and at the times the Superintendent requires,

(a)
identifying all persons duly authorized as its or their agents in the Province,

(b)
identifying all persons to whom it or they have paid or allowed or agreed to pay or allow directly or indirectly, compensation for placing or negotiating insurance on lives, property or interests in the Province, or negotiating the continuance or renewal of the contract, or for attempting to do so, and

(c)
including any information required by the Superintendent.
